Are you a migrant worker? [Click here](https://help.healthserve.org.sg/)

您是客工吗？ [请点击这里。](https://help.healthserve.org.sg/)

நீங்கள் புலம்பெயர்ந்த தொழிலாளியா? [இங்கே
அழுத்தவும்](https://help.healthserve.org.sg/)

আপনি কি একজন অভিবাসী শ্রমিক? [এখানে ক্লিক
করুন।](https://help.healthserve.org.sg/)

သင်သည်တစ်စုံတစ်ဦးနှင့်စကားပြောလိုသော ရွှေ့ပြောင်းအလုပ်သမားတစ်ဦးလား။
[ဤနေရာကိုကလစ်နှိပ်ပါ။](https://help.healthserve.org.sg/)

# We believe in a society where every migrant worker lives a life of health,
well-being and dignity. Do you?

[ Get involved ](/volunteer/)

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-
content/uploads/2022/03/banner2-scaled.jpg)

# Support our migrant community's healthcare needs

[ Make a donation ](https://give.healthserve.org.sg/)

## With our community's support, here's a snapshot of HealthServe's impact in
the past year.

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/migrant-workers-
engaged.svg)

0

### Migrant workers engaged in 2022

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/medical-
consultation.svg)

## 7,700

Medical consultations (across acute, chronic disease management, dental,
rehabilitation and specialist services)

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/mental-health-
helpline.svg)

## 7,100

Migrant workers supported through mental health services (via crisis helpline,
counselling support, mental health education workshops)

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/social-
assistance.svg)

## 3,100

Cases of social assistance rendered (in emergency financial aid, meals,
groceries, phone and transport top-ups)

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/workers-under-
quarantine.svg)

## 13,400

Migrant workers engaged through outreach events and health screenings

[ Learn about our impact ](/our-impact/)

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/registered-
charity.jpg)

### Established in 2006, HealthServe is an IPC registered charity dedicated to
bringing healing and hope to the migrant community in Singapore.

We serve disadvantaged migrant workers through the provision of holistic and
affordable care, from medical and mental health services to casework support
and other forms of social assistance.

[ Learn more about our work ](/medical-dental-services/)

### With your generous donation, we can keep our clinic and healthcare
services running for migrant workers who need support.

Your kind gesture provides healing and hope to low-wage migrant workers in
Singapore. Make a monthly commitment today!

[ Donate ](https://give.healthserve.org.sg/)

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-
content/uploads/2022/03/CCH5559_ByCarolineChia.jpg)

## Hear From Our Community

If we visit [private] clinics, the consultation fee is high and there’s a
language barrier, they can’t understand me. That’s why I came here. For those
people from my hometown with fevers or headaches, I will recommend them to
come here.

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-
content/uploads/2022/03/user_default.png)

Guo

Construction worker from China

HealthServe has made me feel more secure about being in a foreign country and
reminded me not to be afraid or lonely in case I need medical or emotional
support.

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Rona-at-Cruise-
Ship-300x294.jpg)

Rona

Shipyard worker from Bangladesh

I thinking, I no makan but no die, maybe HealthServe come from God to help me.

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-
content/uploads/2022/03/Dipu-300x300.jpg)

Dipu

Construction worker from Bangladesh

HealthServe saved my life.

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Jing-Xiao-
Jiang-300x259.jpg)

Jiang

Waste management worker from China

What I’m most grateful to HealthServe for is... showing me a direction to work
towards, whenever there is something I don’t understand. And when we don’t
receive our rightful compensation, HealthServe mediates for us with the
government and our employers.

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Dong-Hai-
Airport-send-off-300x270.jpg)

Dong

Construction worker from China

HealthServe has been really helpful to me, especially with my medical expenses
and issues

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-
content/uploads/2022/03/dinesh-300x300.jpg)

Dinesh

Factory Worker from India

Everyone here is really friendly and nice, and is always willing to offer a
listening ear

![](https://www.healthserve.org.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/ali-300x300.jpg)

Ali Jamat

Excavator Operator from Bangladesh

# **Do you feel unwell?**

# Visit HealthServe's Clinic @ Geylang

#

1 Lorong 23 Geylang S388352 (Aljunied MRT)  
Clinic Hours: 6.30pm - 9.30pm (Tue, Wed & Thurs)  
Work Permit / S-Pass Holders: SGD8 for Acute diseases, SGD15 for Chronic
Diseases Special Pass Holders: FREE

  
Call/Whatsapp: +65 31574458

## Seeking assistance for a migrant worker?

### +65 3129 5000

HealthServe 24-hour Helpline

Call HealthServe’s 24-hour helpline or email us at:

## Serving the migrant worker community in Singapore since 2006 🇸🇬

[help.healthserve.org.sg](https://www.tiktok.com/link/v2?aid=1988&lang=en&scene=bio_url&target=help.healthserve.org.sg)

![“Mental health is a universal human right.” 🤝 To remind our migrant brothers
of their universal human right, we got together with close to 50 of our Peer
Support Leaders \(PSLs\) last Sunday to commemorate World Mental Health Day!
Through engaging and thought-provoking activities planned by our mental health
team, our PSLs expanded their understanding about resilience and useful stress
management techniques 💪🏽 We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends
stepping forward as volunteers, empowering their fellow brothers. Watch on for
a glimpse of our joyous day 🥰! #migrantworkers #community #HealthServe

**820**](https://www.tiktok.com/)

“Mental health is a universal human right.” 🤝  
  
To remind our migrant brothers of their universal human right, we got together
with close to 50 of our Peer Support Leaders (PSLs) last Sunday to commemorate
World Mental Health Day!  
  
Through engaging and thought-provoking activities planned by our mental health
team, our PSLs expanded their understanding about resilience and useful stress
management techniques 💪🏽  
  
We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends stepping forward as volunteers,
empowering their fellow brothers. Watch on for a glimpse of our joyous day 🥰!  
  
#migrantworkers #community #HealthServe #WorldMentalHealthDay2023
#WorldMentalHealthDay #mentalhealthawareness #mentalhealth #resilience](
"“Mental health is a universal human right.” 🤝 To remind our migrant brothers
of their universal human right, we got together with close to 50 of our Peer
Support Leaders \(PSLs\) last Sunday to commemorate World Mental Health Day!
Through engaging and thought-provoking activities planned by our mental health
team, our PSLs expanded their understanding about resilience and useful stress
management techniques 💪🏽 We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends
stepping forward as volunteers, empowering their fellow brothers. Watch on for

[[ **#DidYouKnow **](/tag/didyouknow) that the number of migrant callers to
HealthServe’s crisis helpline doubled to 4,000 in 2022?  
  
Manned by trained crisis helpline specialists and volunteers, the round-the-
clock service serves to provide a safe space for migrant workers in distress.  
  
This World Suicide Prevention Day, we asked our counsellor Durga about one
call that affected her the most.  
  
You can lend a listening ear too👂🏽: https://healthserve.org.sg/volunteer

[![Curious how a Peer Support Leader \(PSL\) training programme for migrant
workers looks like? Join us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather
every week to conduct uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant
friends, right in their dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬
#DidYouKnow that HealthServe kicked off its first PSL training – the first of
its kind in Singapore for migrant workers – in 2021? To date, we’ve equipped
close to 1100 PSLs who serve as crucial first detectors of distress signs on
the ground. Huge shoutout to our community of participants, supportive
employers and committed volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟 #HealthServe
#CommunityCare #mentalhealth #healthcare #migrantworkers #behindhealthserve
created by HealthServe with HealthServe's original sound -
HealthServe](https://p16-sign-sg.tiktokcdn.com/tos-

[ Curious how a Peer Support Leader (PSL) training programme for migrant
workers looks like?  
  
Join us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather every week to
conduct uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant friends, right in
their dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬  
  
[**#DidYouKnow **](/tag/didyouknow) that HealthServe kicked off its first PSL
training – the first of its kind in Singapore for migrant workers – in 2021?
To date, we’ve equipped close to 1100 PSLs who serve as crucial first
detectors of distress signs on the ground.  
  
Huge shoutout to our community of participants, supportive employers and
committed volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟  
  
[**#HealthServe **](/tag/healthserve) [**#CommunityCare
**](/tag/communitycare) [**#mentalhealth **](/tag/mentalhealth) [**#healthcare
**](/tag/healthcare) [**#migrantworkers **](/tag/migrantworkers)
[**#behindhealthserve **](/tag/behindhealthserve) ]( "Curious how a Peer
Support Leader \(PSL\) training programme for migrant workers looks like? Join
us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather every week to conduct
uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant friends, right in their
dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬 #DidYouKnow that HealthServe
kicked off its first PSL training – the first of its kind in Singapore for
migrant workers – in 2021? To date, we’ve equipped close to 1100 PSLs who
serve as crucial first detectors of distress signs on the ground. Huge
shoutout to our community of participants, supportive employers and committed
volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟 #HealthServe #CommunityCare #mentalhealth
#healthcare #migrantworkers #behindhealthserve ")

[![Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers?  🏥✨
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need. For the past 16
years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill low-wage migrant
workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So thankful for
their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff, volunteers and
interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️ 🕡Please keep in mind
that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and Thursday from 6:30 pm to
9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at 5.30pm on a first come first serve basis.
#HealthServe  #Clinic  #CommunityCare  #healthcare  #migrantworkers created by
HealthServe with HealthServe's original sound - HealthServe](https://p16-sign-
sg.tiktokcdn.com/tos-alisg-p-0037/owE6IBBEVIVuAunkw8CLbfGevCVCTD2gQhiRBE~tplv-

[ Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers? 🏥✨  
  
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need.  
  
For the past 16 years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill
low-wage migrant workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So
thankful for their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff,
volunteers and interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️  
  
🕡Please keep in mind that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and
Thursday from 6:30 pm to 9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at 5.30pm on a first
come first serve basis.  
  
[**#HealthServe **](/tag/healthserve) [**#Clinic **](/tag/clinic)
[**#CommunityCare **](/tag/communitycare) [**#healthcare **](/tag/healthcare)
[**#migrantworkers **](/tag/migrantworkers)]( "Curious what goes on behind a
community clinic for migrant workers?  🏥✨ Come along as we peel back the
curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang, where a community comes together
to care for those in need. For the past 16 years, the HealthServe clinic has
stayed open to support ill low-wage migrant workers who did not have access to
affordable healthcare. So thankful for their trust in us, and our committed
team of clinic staff, volunteers and interns who keep our clinic running day
in night out. ❤️ 🕡Please keep in mind that our clinic is open every Tuesday,
Wednesday, and Thursday from 6:30 pm to 9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at
5.30pm on a first come first serve basis. #HealthServe  #Clinic
#CommunityCare  #healthcare  #migrantworkers")

[![நீங்கள் கடைசியாக எப்போது ஓய்வெடுத்தீர்கள்? வாழ்க்கை சில சமயங்களில் பெரும்
பாதிப்பை ஏற்படுத்தும். ஆரோக்கியமான மனதை வைத்து உங்கள் மன நலத்திற்கு முன்னுரிமை
கொடுக்க சிறிது நேரம் ஒதுக்குங்கள். இந்த வீடியோவில் உள்ள 7 வகையான ஓய்வு பற்றி
அறிய, புலம் பெயர்ந்த சகோதரர்களான @Amaran, @Pandiyan @Selvaraj ஆகியோருடன்
இணையுங்கள் உங்கள் ஆதரவிற்கு எங்கள் தன்னார்வலர்களான Rachmat, Patrick, Arul
ஆகியோருக்கு நன்றி துன்பத்தில் இருக்கும் புலம்பெயர்ந்த தொழிலாளி உங்களுக்குத்
தெரிந்தால், 3129 5000 என்ற எண்ணில் HealthServe ஐ அழைக்கவும். ----- When was
the last time you really rested? Life can get overwhelming at times. Take a
moment to prioritise your mental well-being by keeping a healthy mind.  Join
our migrant brothers @Amaran, @Pandiyan @Selvaraj in learning about the 7
types of rest in this video 😌 Thank you to our volunteers Rachmat, Patrick and
Arul for your support 🎬 ☎️ If you know a migrant worker in distress, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000. #MigrantMatters #HealthServeTips  #CaringforYourMind
#health  #mentalhealth #wellness created by HealthServe with HealthServe's

[ நீங்கள் கடைசியாக எப்போது ஓய்வெடுத்தீர்கள்?  
  
வாழ்க்கை சில சமயங்களில் பெரும் பாதிப்பை ஏற்படுத்தும். ஆரோக்கியமான மனதை வைத்து
உங்கள் மன நலத்திற்கு முன்னுரிமை கொடுக்க சிறிது நேரம் ஒதுக்குங்கள்.  
  
இந்த வீடியோவில் உள்ள 7 வகையான ஓய்வு பற்றி அறிய, புலம் பெயர்ந்த சகோதரர்களான
@Amaran, @Pandiyan @Selvaraj ஆகியோருடன் இணையுங்கள்  
  
உங்கள் ஆதரவிற்கு எங்கள் தன்னார்வலர்களான Rachmat, Patrick, Arul ஆகியோருக்கு
நன்றி  
  
துன்பத்தில் இருக்கும் புலம்பெயர்ந்த தொழிலாளி உங்களுக்குத் தெரிந்தால், 3129
5000 என்ற எண்ணில் HealthServe ஐ அழைக்கவும்.  
\-----  
When was the last time you really rested?  
  
Life can get overwhelming at times. Take a moment to prioritise your mental
well-being by keeping a healthy mind.  
  
Join our migrant brothers @Amaran, @Pandiyan @Selvaraj in learning about the 7
types of rest in this video 😌  
  
Thank you to our volunteers Rachmat, Patrick and Arul for your support 🎬  
  
☎️ If you know a migrant worker in distress, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.

[ আপনি শেষ কবে খুব ভাল করে বিশ্রাম নিয়েছেন?  
  
কোনও কোনও সময় জীবন খুব গতিময় হয়ে ওঠে।  
আপনার মানসিক সুস্থতাকে প্রাধান্য দিতে একটু সময় বের করুন যাতে আপনার মন ভাল
থাকে।  
  
আমাদের অভিবাসী ভাইদের সঙ্গে অংশগ্রহণ করুন এবং এই ভিডিওর মাধ্যমে ৭ রকমের
বিশ্রাম সম্পর্কে শিখুন। 😌  
  
আপনাদের সাহায্যের জন্য ধন্যবাদ ভলান্টিয়ার জুন জি 🎬  
  
☎️আপনার পরিচিত কোনও অভিবাসী কর্মী কষ্টে বা সমস্যায় থাকলে, ফোন করুন হেলথ
সার্ভে : 3129 5000.

well-being by keeping a healthy mind.

Are you feeling back pain?  
We partner our volunteer physiotherapist Ernie to share 3 steps to check your
body, and 3 simple strengthening exercises! 📷📷📷  
Found this video useful? Share it with your friends and try these together!  
If you still feel pain or need help, remember to call HealthServe’s 24-hour
helpline at 3129 5000.  
Special thanks to One Physio and our sporting migrant brothers Rajiv Krishna
Kanthan Raman 📷

[ আপনি কি আপনার পিঠে ব্যথা অনুভব করছেন?  
আমরা আমাদের স্বেচ্ছাসেবক ফিজিওথেরাপিস্ট ERNIE কে আপনার শরীর পরীক্ষা করার জন্য
৩ টি ধাপ এবং ৩ টি সহজ ব্যায়াম শরীর শক্তিশালী করার জন্য শেয়ার করতে অংশ নিতে
বলি! 📷📷📷  
এই ভিডিওটি কি আপনার দরকারী মনে হয় ? তাহলে আপনার বন্ধুদের সাথে শেয়ার করুন এবং
একসাথে এটি করার চেষ্টা করুন!  
আপনি যদি এর পরেও ব্যথা অনুভব করেন বা সাহায্যের প্রয়োজন হয়, তাহলে 3129 5000
এই নম্বরে HealthServe-এর হেল্পলাইনে কল করতে ভুলবেন না, এটি ২৪ ঘন্টা খোলা থাকে।  
One Physio এবং আমাদের স্পোর্টিং অভিবাসী ভাইদেরকে বিশেষ ধন্যবাদ Juel Rana,
Gaurhari Mondal 📷

body, and 3 simple strengthening exercises! 📷📷📷

ব্যায়াম  শরীর শক্তিশালী  করার জন্য শেয়ার করতে অংশ নিতে বলি!  📷📷📷 এই ভিডিওটি
কি আপনার দরকারী মনে হয় ? তাহলে  আপনার বন্ধুদের সাথে শেয়ার করুন এবং একসাথে
এটি করার চেষ্টা করুন! আপনি যদি এর পরেও ব্যথা অনুভব করেন বা সাহায্যের প্রয়োজন
হয়, তাহলে 3129 5000 এই নম্বরে HealthServe-এর হেল্পলাইনে কল করতে ভুলবেন না,
এটি ২৪ ঘন্টা খোলা থাকে। One Physio  এবং আমাদের স্পোর্টিং অভিবাসী ভাইদেরকে
বিশেষ ধন্যবাদ Juel Rana, Gaurhari Mondal 📷 ---- Are you feeling back pain? We
partner our volunteer physiotherapist Ernie to share 3 steps to check your
body, and 3 simple strengthening exercises! 📷📷📷 Found this video useful? Share
it with your friends and try these together! If you still feel pain or need
help, remember to call HealthServe’s 24-hour helpline at 3129 5000. Special
thanks to One Physio and our sporting migrant brothers Juel Rana, Gaurhari
Mondal 📷 #MigrantMatters #HealthServeTips #CaringforYourHeart #health
#mentalhealth #wellness")

[![சொந்த நாட்டை விட்டு, வேறு ஒரு நாட்டில் வாழ்க்கையை வழிநடத்துவது சவாலானது
மற்றும் ஒருவரை பெரும்பாலும் தனிமைப்படுத்த வாய்ப்பு உள்ளது.  இந்த
#internationalmenshealthweek, ஹெல்த்சர்வின் புலம்பெயர்ந்த நண்பர்களைக் கொண்ட
எங்கள் மூன்று-அத்தியாய தொடரான #MigrantMatters -யின் முதல் அத்தியாயத்தை நாங்கள்
வெளியிடுகிறோம். அவர்கள் பயணித்த வாழ்க்கைப் பாதைகள் கடினமானவை, மேலும் அவர்களின்
ஆழ்ந்த தனிப்பட்ட கதைகளை எங்களுடனும், மற்றும் எங்கள் மத்தியில் உள்ள
பல்லாயிரக்கணக்கான குறைந்த ஊதியம் பெறும் புலம்பெயர்ந்த தொழிலாளர்களுடனும்,
பகிர்ந்துக் கொண்ட அவர்களுக்கு நாங்கள் நன்றி தெரிவிக்கிறோம்.  📞புலம்பெயர்ந்த
தொழிலாளி ஒருவரைப் பற்றி உங்களுக்குத் தெரிந்தால், அவர்களுடன் பேசுவதற்கு யாராவது
தேவைப்படலாம், 3129 5000 என்ற எண்ணில் HealthServe-யை அழைக்கவும்.    தாயகத்தில்
தங்களுடைய குடும்பங்களுக்கு உதவ தன்னலமின்றியும் அயராது உழைக்கும் புலம்பெயர்ந்த
சகோதரர்கள் அனைவருக்கும் தந்தையர் தின நல்வாழ்த்துக்கள் 👨❤️ அடுத்த வார இறுதியில்

Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  This
#InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode series
#MigrantMatters, featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan,
Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are grateful to them
for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and the tens of
thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.   📞If you know of a
migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.

and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  Stay tuned for the

\-----  
Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This #InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode
series [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s
migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan, Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been
rough, and we are grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal
stories with us and the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our
midst.  
  
📞If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  
  
Stay tuned for the next episode of [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters)
next weekend!

**](/tag/migrantmatters)]( "বাড়ি থেকে দূরের জীবন  চ্যালেঞ্জিং এবং প্রায়শই
পরিবারের সাথে যোগাযোগ বিচ্ছিন্ন হতে পারে। এই #InternationalMensHealthWeek,
আমরা HealthServe-এর অভিবাসী বন্ধুদের Imon , Samim,  Juel Rana  সমন্বিত
MigrantMatters-এর তিন পর্বের সিরিজের প্রথমটি উন্মোচন করেছি ।  তাদের রাস্তাগুলি
রুক্ষ ছিল, এবং আমাদের সাথে তাদের গভীর ব্যক্তিগত গল্প শেয়ার করা এবং আমাদের মাঝে
হাজার হাজার স্বল্প বেতনের অভিবাসী শ্রমিকদের সাহসের সাথে ভাগ করে নেওয়ার জন্য
আমরা তাদের কাছে কৃতজ্ঞ। ☎️আপনি যদি একজন অভিবাসী কর্মী সম্পর্কে জানেন যার সাথে
কথা বলার জন্য কারো প্রয়োজন হতে পারে, তাহলে 3129 5000 নম্বরে HealthServe-এ কল
করুন। আমাদের সমস্ত অভিবাসী ভাইদের জন্য বাবা দিবসের শুভেচ্ছা , যারা তাদের
পরিবারের জন্য নিঃস্বার্থভাবে এবং নিরলসভাবে কাজ করে।👨🏻❤️ পরের সপ্তাহান্তে
#MigrantMatters  -এর পরবর্তী পর্বের জন্য সাথে থাকুন! ----------- Navigating
life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating. This
#Internationalmenshealthweek , we unveil the first of our three-episode series
#MigrantMatters, featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Imon , Samim, and
Juel Rana. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are grateful to them
for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and the tens of
thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst. ☎️ If you know of a
migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨🏻❤️ Stay tuned for the
next episode of #MigrantMattersnext weekend! #MigrantMatters #HealthServeTips
#CaringforYourHeart #health #mentalhealth #wellness")

management techniques 💪🏽 We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends

“Mental health is a universal human right.” 🤝  
  
To remind our migrant brothers of their universal human right, we got together
with close to 50 of our Peer Support Leaders (PSLs) last Sunday to commemorate
World Mental Health Day!  
  
Through engaging and thought-provoking activities planned by our mental health
team, our PSLs expanded their understanding about resilience and useful stress
management techniques 💪🏽  
  
We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends stepping forward as volunteers,
empowering their fellow brothers. Watch on for a glimpse of our joyous day 🥰!  
  
#migrantworkers #community #HealthServe #WorldMentalHealthDay2023
#WorldMentalHealthDay #mentalhealthawareness #mentalhealth #resilience](

[![Curious how a Peer Support Leader \(PSL\) training programme for migrant
workers looks like? Join us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather
every week to conduct uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant
friends, right in their dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬
#DidYouKnow that HealthServe kicked off its first PSL training – the first of
its kind in Singapore for migrant workers – in 2021? To date, we’ve equipped
close to 1100 PSLs who serve as crucial first detectors of distress signs on
the ground. Huge shoutout to our community of participants, supportive
employers and committed volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟 #HealthServe
#CommunityCare #mentalhealth #healthcare #migrantworkers #behindhealthserve

[ Curious how a Peer Support Leader (PSL) training programme for migrant
workers looks like?  
  
Join us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather every week to
conduct uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant friends, right in
their dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬  
  
[**#DidYouKnow **](/tag/didyouknow) that HealthServe kicked off its first PSL
training – the first of its kind in Singapore for migrant workers – in 2021?
To date, we’ve equipped close to 1100 PSLs who serve as crucial first
detectors of distress signs on the ground.  
  
Huge shoutout to our community of participants, supportive employers and
committed volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟

[![Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers?  🏥✨
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need. For the past 16
years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill low-wage migrant
workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So thankful for
their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff, volunteers and
interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️ 🕡Please keep in mind
that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and Thursday from 6:30 pm to
9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at 5.30pm on a first come first serve basis.
#HealthServe  #Clinic  #CommunityCare  #healthcare  #migrantworkers created by
HealthServe with HealthServe's original sound - HealthServe](https://p16-sign-

[ Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers? 🏥✨  
  
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need.  
  
For the past 16 years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill
low-wage migrant workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So
thankful for their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff,
volunteers and interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️  
  
🕡Please keep in mind that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and
Thursday from 6:30 pm to 9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at 5.30pm on a first
come first serve basis.

[**#CommunityCare **](/tag/communitycare) [**#healthcare **](/tag/healthcare)
[**#migrantworkers **](/tag/migrantworkers)]( "Curious what goes on behind a
community clinic for migrant workers?  🏥✨ Come along as we peel back the
curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang, where a community comes together
to care for those in need. For the past 16 years, the HealthServe clinic has
stayed open to support ill low-wage migrant workers who did not have access to
affordable healthcare. So thankful for their trust in us, and our committed
team of clinic staff, volunteers and interns who keep our clinic running day
in night out. ❤️ 🕡Please keep in mind that our clinic is open every Tuesday,
Wednesday, and Thursday from 6:30 pm to 9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at

[ আপনি কি আপনার পিঠে ব্যথা অনুভব করছেন?  
আমরা আমাদের স্বেচ্ছাসেবক ফিজিওথেরাপিস্ট ERNIE কে আপনার শরীর পরীক্ষা করার জন্য
৩ টি ধাপ এবং ৩ টি সহজ ব্যায়াম শরীর শক্তিশালী করার জন্য শেয়ার করতে অংশ নিতে
বলি! 📷📷📷  
এই ভিডিওটি কি আপনার দরকারী মনে হয় ? তাহলে আপনার বন্ধুদের সাথে শেয়ার করুন এবং
একসাথে এটি করার চেষ্টা করুন!  
আপনি যদি এর পরেও ব্যথা অনুভব করেন বা সাহায্যের প্রয়োজন হয়, তাহলে 3129 5000
এই নম্বরে HealthServe-এর হেল্পলাইনে কল করতে ভুলবেন না, এটি ২৪ ঘন্টা খোলা থাকে।  
One Physio এবং আমাদের স্পোর্টিং অভিবাসী ভাইদেরকে বিশেষ ধন্যবাদ Juel Rana,
Gaurhari Mondal 📷  
\----  
Are you feeling back pain?  
We partner our volunteer physiotherapist Ernie to share 3 steps to check your
body, and 3 simple strengthening exercises! 📷📷📷  
Found this video useful? Share it with your friends and try these together!  
If you still feel pain or need help, remember to call HealthServe’s 24-hour
helpline at 3129 5000.  
Special thanks to One Physio and our sporting migrant brothers Juel Rana,
Gaurhari Mondal  
📷

மற்றும் ஒருவரை பெரும்பாலும் தனிமைப்படுத்த வாய்ப்பு உள்ளது.  இந்த

பகிர்ந்துக் கொண்ட அவர்களுக்கு நாங்கள் நன்றி தெரிவிக்கிறோம்.  📞புலம்பெயர்ந்த
தொழிலாளி ஒருவரைப் பற்றி உங்களுக்குத் தெரிந்தால், அவர்களுடன் பேசுவதற்கு யாராவது

Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  This
#InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode series
#MigrantMatters, featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan,
Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are grateful to them
for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and the tens of
thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.   📞If you know of a
migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  Stay tuned for the
next episode of #MigrantMatters next weekend!  #MigrantMatters

\-----  
Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This #InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode
series [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s
migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan, Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been
rough, and we are grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal
stories with us and the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our
midst.  
  
📞If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  
  
Stay tuned for the next episode of [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters)
next weekend!

সাথে তাদের গভীর ব্যক্তিগত গল্প শেয়ার করা এবং আমাদের মাঝে হাজার হাজার স্বল্প
বেতনের অভিবাসী শ্রমিকদের সাহসের সাথে ভাগ করে নেওয়ার জন্য আমরা তাদের কাছে
কৃতজ্ঞ। ☎️আপনি যদি একজন অভিবাসী কর্মী সম্পর্কে জানেন যার সাথে কথা বলার জন্য
কারো প্রয়োজন হতে পারে, তাহলে 3129 5000 নম্বরে HealthServe-এ কল করুন। আমাদের
সমস্ত অভিবাসী ভাইদের জন্য বাবা দিবসের শুভেচ্ছা , যারা তাদের পরিবারের জন্য
নিঃস্বার্থভাবে এবং নিরলসভাবে কাজ করে।👨🏻❤️ পরের সপ্তাহান্তে #MigrantMatters

বিচ্ছিন্ন হতে পারে।  
  
এই [**#InternationalMensHealthWeek **](/tag/internationalmenshealthweek), আমরা
HealthServe-এর অভিবাসী বন্ধুদের Imon , Samim, Juel Rana সমন্বিত
MigrantMatters-এর তিন পর্বের সিরিজের প্রথমটি উন্মোচন করেছি । তাদের রাস্তাগুলি
রুক্ষ ছিল, এবং আমাদের সাথে তাদের গভীর ব্যক্তিগত গল্প শেয়ার করা এবং আমাদের মাঝে
হাজার হাজার স্বল্প বেতনের অভিবাসী শ্রমিকদের সাহসের সাথে ভাগ করে নেওয়ার জন্য
আমরা তাদের কাছে কৃতজ্ঞ।  
  
☎️আপনি যদি একজন অভিবাসী কর্মী সম্পর্কে জানেন যার সাথে কথা বলার জন্য কারো
প্রয়োজন হতে পারে, তাহলে 3129 5000 নম্বরে HealthServe-এ কল করুন।  
  
আমাদের সমস্ত অভিবাসী ভাইদের জন্য বাবা দিবসের শুভেচ্ছা , যারা তাদের পরিবারের
জন্য নিঃস্বার্থভাবে এবং নিরলসভাবে কাজ করে।👨🏻❤️  
  
পরের সপ্তাহান্তে [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters) -এর পরবর্তী
পর্বের জন্য সাথে থাকুন!  
\-----------  
Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This [**#Internationalmenshealthweek **](/tag/internationalmenshealthweek) ,
we unveil the first of our three-episode series [**#MigrantMatters
**](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Imon ,
Samim, and Juel Rana. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are
grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and
the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.  
  
☎️ If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨🏻❤️  
  
Stay tuned for the next episode of [**#MigrantMatters
**](/tag/migrantmatters)next weekend!  
  
#MigrantMatters [**#HealthServeTips **](/tag/healthservetips)

পরিবারের সাথে যোগাযোগ বিচ্ছিন্ন হতে পারে। এই #InternationalMensHealthWeek,
আমরা HealthServe-এর অভিবাসী বন্ধুদের Imon , Samim,  Juel Rana  সমন্বিত

“Mental health is a universal human right.” 🤝  
  
To remind our migrant brothers of their universal human right, we got together
with close to 50 of our Peer Support Leaders (PSLs) last Sunday to commemorate
World Mental Health Day!  
  
Through engaging and thought-provoking activities planned by our mental health
team, our PSLs expanded their understanding about resilience and useful stress
management techniques 💪🏽  
  
We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends stepping forward as volunteers,
empowering their fellow brothers. Watch on for a glimpse of our joyous day 🥰!  
  
#migrantworkers #community #HealthServe #WorldMentalHealthDay2023
#WorldMentalHealthDay #mentalhealthawareness #mentalhealth #resilience](

[![Curious how a Peer Support Leader \(PSL\) training programme for migrant
workers looks like? Join us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather
every week to conduct uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant
friends, right in their dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬
#DidYouKnow that HealthServe kicked off its first PSL training – the first of
its kind in Singapore for migrant workers – in 2021? To date, we’ve equipped
close to 1100 PSLs who serve as crucial first detectors of distress signs on
the ground. Huge shoutout to our community of participants, supportive
employers and committed volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟 #HealthServe

[ Curious how a Peer Support Leader (PSL) training programme for migrant
workers looks like?  
  
Join us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather every week to
conduct uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant friends, right in
their dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬  
  
[**#DidYouKnow **](/tag/didyouknow) that HealthServe kicked off its first PSL
training – the first of its kind in Singapore for migrant workers – in 2021?
To date, we’ve equipped close to 1100 PSLs who serve as crucial first
detectors of distress signs on the ground.  
  
Huge shoutout to our community of participants, supportive employers and
committed volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟

[![Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers?  🏥✨
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need. For the past 16
years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill low-wage migrant
workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So thankful for
their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff, volunteers and
interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️ 🕡Please keep in mind
that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and Thursday from 6:30 pm to
9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at 5.30pm on a first come first serve basis.

[ Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers? 🏥✨  
  
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need.  
  
For the past 16 years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill
low-wage migrant workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So
thankful for their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff,
volunteers and interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️  
  
🕡Please keep in mind that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and
Thursday from 6:30 pm to 9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at 5.30pm on a first
come first serve basis.

কোনও কোনও সময় জীবন খুব গতিময় হয়ে ওঠে।

Are you feeling back pain?  
We partner our volunteer physiotherapist Ernie to share 3 steps to check your
body, and 3 simple strengthening exercises! 📷📷📷  
Found this video useful? Share it with your friends and try these together!  
If you still feel pain or need help, remember to call HealthServe’s 24-hour
helpline at 3129 5000.

எங்கள் மூன்று-அத்தியாய தொடரான #MigrantMatters -யின் முதல் அத்தியாயத்தை நாங்கள்

பகிர்ந்துக் கொண்ட அவர்களுக்கு நாங்கள் நன்றி தெரிவிக்கிறோம்.  📞புலம்பெயர்ந்த

Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  This
#InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode series
#MigrantMatters, featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan,
Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are grateful to them
for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and the tens of
thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.   📞If you know of a
migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  Stay tuned for the
next episode of #MigrantMatters next weekend!  #MigrantMatters

Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This #InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode
series [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s
migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan, Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been
rough, and we are grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal
stories with us and the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our
midst.  
  
📞If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  
  
Stay tuned for the next episode of [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters)
next weekend!

[ বাড়ি থেকে দূরের জীবন চ্যালেঞ্জিং এবং প্রায়শই পরিবারের সাথে যোগাযোগ
বিচ্ছিন্ন হতে পারে।  
  
এই [**#InternationalMensHealthWeek **](/tag/internationalmenshealthweek), আমরা
HealthServe-এর অভিবাসী বন্ধুদের Imon , Samim, Juel Rana সমন্বিত
MigrantMatters-এর তিন পর্বের সিরিজের প্রথমটি উন্মোচন করেছি । তাদের রাস্তাগুলি
রুক্ষ ছিল, এবং আমাদের সাথে তাদের গভীর ব্যক্তিগত গল্প শেয়ার করা এবং আমাদের মাঝে
হাজার হাজার স্বল্প বেতনের অভিবাসী শ্রমিকদের সাহসের সাথে ভাগ করে নেওয়ার জন্য
আমরা তাদের কাছে কৃতজ্ঞ।  
  
☎️আপনি যদি একজন অভিবাসী কর্মী সম্পর্কে জানেন যার সাথে কথা বলার জন্য কারো
প্রয়োজন হতে পারে, তাহলে 3129 5000 নম্বরে HealthServe-এ কল করুন।  
  
আমাদের সমস্ত অভিবাসী ভাইদের জন্য বাবা দিবসের শুভেচ্ছা , যারা তাদের পরিবারের
জন্য নিঃস্বার্থভাবে এবং নিরলসভাবে কাজ করে।👨🏻❤️  
  
পরের সপ্তাহান্তে [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters) -এর পরবর্তী
পর্বের জন্য সাথে থাকুন!  
\-----------  
Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This [**#Internationalmenshealthweek **](/tag/internationalmenshealthweek) ,
we unveil the first of our three-episode series [**#MigrantMatters
**](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Imon ,
Samim, and Juel Rana. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are
grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and
the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.  
  
☎️ If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨🏻❤️  
  
Stay tuned for the next episode of [**#MigrantMatters
**](/tag/migrantmatters)next weekend!

পরিবারের সাথে যোগাযোগ বিচ্ছিন্ন হতে পারে। এই #InternationalMensHealthWeek,

হাজার হাজার স্বল্প বেতনের অভিবাসী শ্রমিকদের সাহসের সাথে ভাগ করে নেওয়ার জন্য

“Mental health is a universal human right.” 🤝  
  
To remind our migrant brothers of their universal human right, we got together
with close to 50 of our Peer Support Leaders (PSLs) last Sunday to commemorate
World Mental Health Day!  
  
Through engaging and thought-provoking activities planned by our mental health
team, our PSLs expanded their understanding about resilience and useful stress
management techniques 💪🏽  
  
We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends stepping forward as volunteers,
empowering their fellow brothers. Watch on for a glimpse of our joyous day 🥰!  
  
#migrantworkers #community #HealthServe #WorldMentalHealthDay2023
#WorldMentalHealthDay #mentalhealthawareness #mentalhealth #resilience](

[[ **#DidYouKnow **](/tag/didyouknow) that the number of migrant callers to
HealthServe’s crisis helpline doubled to 4,000 in 2022?  
  
Manned by trained crisis helpline specialists and volunteers, the round-the-
clock service serves to provide a safe space for migrant workers in distress.  
  
This World Suicide Prevention Day, we asked our counsellor Durga about one
call that affected her the most.  
  
You can lend a listening ear too👂🏽: https://healthserve.org.sg/volunteer

[![Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers?  🏥✨
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need. For the past 16
years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill low-wage migrant
workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So thankful for
their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff, volunteers and
interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️ 🕡Please keep in mind
that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and Thursday from 6:30 pm to
9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at 5.30pm on a first come first serve basis.

volunteers and interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️

[ আপনি শেষ কবে খুব ভাল করে বিশ্রাম নিয়েছেন?  
  
কোনও কোনও সময় জীবন খুব গতিময় হয়ে ওঠে।  
আপনার মানসিক সুস্থতাকে প্রাধান্য দিতে একটু সময় বের করুন যাতে আপনার মন ভাল
থাকে।  
  
আমাদের অভিবাসী ভাইদের সঙ্গে অংশগ্রহণ করুন এবং এই ভিডিওর মাধ্যমে ৭ রকমের
বিশ্রাম সম্পর্কে শিখুন। 😌  
  
আপনাদের সাহায্যের জন্য ধন্যবাদ ভলান্টিয়ার জুন জি 🎬  
  
☎️আপনার পরিচিত কোনও অভিবাসী কর্মী কষ্টে বা সমস্যায় থাকলে, ফোন করুন হেলথ
সার্ভে : 3129 5000.

দিতে একটু সময় বের করুন যাতে আপনার মন ভাল থাকে।  আমাদের অভিবাসী ভাইদের সঙ্গে
অংশগ্রহণ করুন এবং এই ভিডিওর মাধ্যমে ৭ রকমের বিশ্রাম সম্পর্কে শিখুন।  😌 আপনাদের
সাহায্যের জন্য ধন্যবাদ ভলান্টিয়ার জুন জি  🎬 ☎️আপনার পরিচিত কোনও অভিবাসী কর্মী
কষ্টে বা সমস্যায় থাকলে, ফোন করুন হেলথ সার্ভে : 3129 5000. ----- When was the
last time you really rested? Life can get overwhelming at times. Take a moment
to prioritise your mental well-being by keeping a healthy mind.  Join our
migrant brothers @Hasan Samim, @Masud and @Riyad in learning about the 7 types
of rest in this video 😌 Thank you to our volunteers Jun Jie, Nazmul, and
Farick for your support 🎬 ☎️ If you know a migrant worker in distress, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000. #MigrantMatters #HealthServeTips  #CaringforYourMind
#health  #mentalhealth  #wellness")

பகிர்ந்துக் கொண்ட அவர்களுக்கு நாங்கள் நன்றி தெரிவிக்கிறோம்.  📞புலம்பெயர்ந்த

Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  This
#InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode series
#MigrantMatters, featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan,
Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are grateful to them
for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and the tens of
thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.   📞If you know of a
migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  Stay tuned for the
next episode of #MigrantMatters next weekend!  #MigrantMatters

Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This #InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode
series [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s
migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan, Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been
rough, and we are grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal
stories with us and the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our
midst.  
  
📞If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  
  
Stay tuned for the next episode of [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters)
next weekend!

সাথে তাদের গভীর ব্যক্তিগত গল্প শেয়ার করা এবং আমাদের মাঝে হাজার হাজার স্বল্প

রুক্ষ ছিল, এবং আমাদের সাথে তাদের গভীর ব্যক্তিগত গল্প শেয়ার করা এবং আমাদের মাঝে

প্রয়োজন হতে পারে, তাহলে 3129 5000 নম্বরে HealthServe-এ কল করুন।

জন্য নিঃস্বার্থভাবে এবং নিরলসভাবে কাজ করে।👨🏻❤️

\-----------  
Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This [**#Internationalmenshealthweek **](/tag/internationalmenshealthweek) ,
we unveil the first of our three-episode series [**#MigrantMatters
**](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Imon ,
Samim, and Juel Rana. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are
grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and
the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.  
  
☎️ If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨🏻❤️  
  
Stay tuned for the next episode of [**#MigrantMatters
**](/tag/migrantmatters)next weekend!

## Serving the migrant worker community in Singapore since 2006 🇸🇬

[help.healthserve.org.sg](https://www.tiktok.com/link/v2?aid=1988&lang=en&scene=bio_url&target=help.healthserve.org.sg)

![“Mental health is a universal human right.” 🤝 To remind our migrant brothers
of their universal human right, we got together with close to 50 of our Peer
Support Leaders \(PSLs\) last Sunday to commemorate World Mental Health Day!
Through engaging and thought-provoking activities planned by our mental health
team, our PSLs expanded their understanding about resilience and useful stress
management techniques 💪🏽 We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends
stepping forward as volunteers, empowering their fellow brothers. Watch on for
a glimpse of our joyous day 🥰! #migrantworkers #community #HealthServe

**820**](https://www.tiktok.com/)

“Mental health is a universal human right.” 🤝  
  
To remind our migrant brothers of their universal human right, we got together
with close to 50 of our Peer Support Leaders (PSLs) last Sunday to commemorate
World Mental Health Day!  
  
Through engaging and thought-provoking activities planned by our mental health
team, our PSLs expanded their understanding about resilience and useful stress
management techniques 💪🏽  
  
We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends stepping forward as volunteers,
empowering their fellow brothers. Watch on for a glimpse of our joyous day 🥰!  
  
#migrantworkers #community #HealthServe #WorldMentalHealthDay2023
#WorldMentalHealthDay #mentalhealthawareness #mentalhealth #resilience](
"“Mental health is a universal human right.” 🤝 To remind our migrant brothers
of their universal human right, we got together with close to 50 of our Peer
Support Leaders \(PSLs\) last Sunday to commemorate World Mental Health Day!
Through engaging and thought-provoking activities planned by our mental health
team, our PSLs expanded their understanding about resilience and useful stress
management techniques 💪🏽 We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends
stepping forward as volunteers, empowering their fellow brothers. Watch on for

[[ **#DidYouKnow **](/tag/didyouknow) that the number of migrant callers to
HealthServe’s crisis helpline doubled to 4,000 in 2022?  
  
Manned by trained crisis helpline specialists and volunteers, the round-the-
clock service serves to provide a safe space for migrant workers in distress.  
  
This World Suicide Prevention Day, we asked our counsellor Durga about one
call that affected her the most.  
  
You can lend a listening ear too👂🏽: https://healthserve.org.sg/volunteer

[![Curious how a Peer Support Leader \(PSL\) training programme for migrant
workers looks like? Join us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather
every week to conduct uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant
friends, right in their dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬
#DidYouKnow that HealthServe kicked off its first PSL training – the first of
its kind in Singapore for migrant workers – in 2021? To date, we’ve equipped
close to 1100 PSLs who serve as crucial first detectors of distress signs on
the ground. Huge shoutout to our community of participants, supportive
employers and committed volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟 #HealthServe
#CommunityCare #mentalhealth #healthcare #migrantworkers #behindhealthserve
created by HealthServe with HealthServe's original sound -
HealthServe](https://p16-sign-sg.tiktokcdn.com/tos-

[ Curious how a Peer Support Leader (PSL) training programme for migrant
workers looks like?  
  
Join us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather every week to
conduct uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant friends, right in
their dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬  
  
[**#DidYouKnow **](/tag/didyouknow) that HealthServe kicked off its first PSL
training – the first of its kind in Singapore for migrant workers – in 2021?
To date, we’ve equipped close to 1100 PSLs who serve as crucial first
detectors of distress signs on the ground.  
  
Huge shoutout to our community of participants, supportive employers and
committed volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟  
  
[**#HealthServe **](/tag/healthserve) [**#CommunityCare
**](/tag/communitycare) [**#mentalhealth **](/tag/mentalhealth) [**#healthcare
**](/tag/healthcare) [**#migrantworkers **](/tag/migrantworkers)
[**#behindhealthserve **](/tag/behindhealthserve) ]( "Curious how a Peer
Support Leader \(PSL\) training programme for migrant workers looks like? Join
us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather every week to conduct
uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant friends, right in their
dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬 #DidYouKnow that HealthServe
kicked off its first PSL training – the first of its kind in Singapore for
migrant workers – in 2021? To date, we’ve equipped close to 1100 PSLs who
serve as crucial first detectors of distress signs on the ground. Huge
shoutout to our community of participants, supportive employers and committed
volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟 #HealthServe #CommunityCare #mentalhealth
#healthcare #migrantworkers #behindhealthserve ")

[![Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers?  🏥✨
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need. For the past 16
years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill low-wage migrant
workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So thankful for
their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff, volunteers and
interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️ 🕡Please keep in mind
that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and Thursday from 6:30 pm to
9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at 5.30pm on a first come first serve basis.
#HealthServe  #Clinic  #CommunityCare  #healthcare  #migrantworkers created by
HealthServe with HealthServe's original sound - HealthServe](https://p16-sign-
sg.tiktokcdn.com/tos-alisg-p-0037/owE6IBBEVIVuAunkw8CLbfGevCVCTD2gQhiRBE~tplv-

[ Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers? 🏥✨  
  
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need.  
  
For the past 16 years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill
low-wage migrant workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So
thankful for their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff,
volunteers and interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️  
  
🕡Please keep in mind that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and
Thursday from 6:30 pm to 9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at 5.30pm on a first
come first serve basis.  
  
[**#HealthServe **](/tag/healthserve) [**#Clinic **](/tag/clinic)
[**#CommunityCare **](/tag/communitycare) [**#healthcare **](/tag/healthcare)
[**#migrantworkers **](/tag/migrantworkers)]( "Curious what goes on behind a
community clinic for migrant workers?  🏥✨ Come along as we peel back the
curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang, where a community comes together
to care for those in need. For the past 16 years, the HealthServe clinic has
stayed open to support ill low-wage migrant workers who did not have access to
affordable healthcare. So thankful for their trust in us, and our committed
team of clinic staff, volunteers and interns who keep our clinic running day
in night out. ❤️ 🕡Please keep in mind that our clinic is open every Tuesday,
Wednesday, and Thursday from 6:30 pm to 9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at
5.30pm on a first come first serve basis. #HealthServe  #Clinic
#CommunityCare  #healthcare  #migrantworkers")

[![நீங்கள் கடைசியாக எப்போது ஓய்வெடுத்தீர்கள்? வாழ்க்கை சில சமயங்களில் பெரும்
பாதிப்பை ஏற்படுத்தும். ஆரோக்கியமான மனதை வைத்து உங்கள் மன நலத்திற்கு முன்னுரிமை
கொடுக்க சிறிது நேரம் ஒதுக்குங்கள். இந்த வீடியோவில் உள்ள 7 வகையான ஓய்வு பற்றி
அறிய, புலம் பெயர்ந்த சகோதரர்களான @Amaran, @Pandiyan @Selvaraj ஆகியோருடன்
இணையுங்கள் உங்கள் ஆதரவிற்கு எங்கள் தன்னார்வலர்களான Rachmat, Patrick, Arul
ஆகியோருக்கு நன்றி துன்பத்தில் இருக்கும் புலம்பெயர்ந்த தொழிலாளி உங்களுக்குத்
தெரிந்தால், 3129 5000 என்ற எண்ணில் HealthServe ஐ அழைக்கவும். ----- When was
the last time you really rested? Life can get overwhelming at times. Take a
moment to prioritise your mental well-being by keeping a healthy mind.  Join
our migrant brothers @Amaran, @Pandiyan @Selvaraj in learning about the 7
types of rest in this video 😌 Thank you to our volunteers Rachmat, Patrick and
Arul for your support 🎬 ☎️ If you know a migrant worker in distress, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000. #MigrantMatters #HealthServeTips  #CaringforYourMind
#health  #mentalhealth #wellness created by HealthServe with HealthServe's

[ நீங்கள் கடைசியாக எப்போது ஓய்வெடுத்தீர்கள்?  
  
வாழ்க்கை சில சமயங்களில் பெரும் பாதிப்பை ஏற்படுத்தும். ஆரோக்கியமான மனதை வைத்து
உங்கள் மன நலத்திற்கு முன்னுரிமை கொடுக்க சிறிது நேரம் ஒதுக்குங்கள்.  
  
இந்த வீடியோவில் உள்ள 7 வகையான ஓய்வு பற்றி அறிய, புலம் பெயர்ந்த சகோதரர்களான
@Amaran, @Pandiyan @Selvaraj ஆகியோருடன் இணையுங்கள்  
  
உங்கள் ஆதரவிற்கு எங்கள் தன்னார்வலர்களான Rachmat, Patrick, Arul ஆகியோருக்கு
நன்றி  
  
துன்பத்தில் இருக்கும் புலம்பெயர்ந்த தொழிலாளி உங்களுக்குத் தெரிந்தால், 3129
5000 என்ற எண்ணில் HealthServe ஐ அழைக்கவும்.  
\-----  
When was the last time you really rested?  
  
Life can get overwhelming at times. Take a moment to prioritise your mental
well-being by keeping a healthy mind.  
  
Join our migrant brothers @Amaran, @Pandiyan @Selvaraj in learning about the 7
types of rest in this video 😌  
  
Thank you to our volunteers Rachmat, Patrick and Arul for your support 🎬  
  
☎️ If you know a migrant worker in distress, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.

[ আপনি শেষ কবে খুব ভাল করে বিশ্রাম নিয়েছেন?  
  
কোনও কোনও সময় জীবন খুব গতিময় হয়ে ওঠে।  
আপনার মানসিক সুস্থতাকে প্রাধান্য দিতে একটু সময় বের করুন যাতে আপনার মন ভাল
থাকে।  
  
আমাদের অভিবাসী ভাইদের সঙ্গে অংশগ্রহণ করুন এবং এই ভিডিওর মাধ্যমে ৭ রকমের
বিশ্রাম সম্পর্কে শিখুন। 😌  
  
আপনাদের সাহায্যের জন্য ধন্যবাদ ভলান্টিয়ার জুন জি 🎬  
  
☎️আপনার পরিচিত কোনও অভিবাসী কর্মী কষ্টে বা সমস্যায় থাকলে, ফোন করুন হেলথ
সার্ভে : 3129 5000.

well-being by keeping a healthy mind.

Are you feeling back pain?  
We partner our volunteer physiotherapist Ernie to share 3 steps to check your
body, and 3 simple strengthening exercises! 📷📷📷  
Found this video useful? Share it with your friends and try these together!  
If you still feel pain or need help, remember to call HealthServe’s 24-hour
helpline at 3129 5000.  
Special thanks to One Physio and our sporting migrant brothers Rajiv Krishna
Kanthan Raman 📷

[ আপনি কি আপনার পিঠে ব্যথা অনুভব করছেন?  
আমরা আমাদের স্বেচ্ছাসেবক ফিজিওথেরাপিস্ট ERNIE কে আপনার শরীর পরীক্ষা করার জন্য
৩ টি ধাপ এবং ৩ টি সহজ ব্যায়াম শরীর শক্তিশালী করার জন্য শেয়ার করতে অংশ নিতে
বলি! 📷📷📷  
এই ভিডিওটি কি আপনার দরকারী মনে হয় ? তাহলে আপনার বন্ধুদের সাথে শেয়ার করুন এবং
একসাথে এটি করার চেষ্টা করুন!  
আপনি যদি এর পরেও ব্যথা অনুভব করেন বা সাহায্যের প্রয়োজন হয়, তাহলে 3129 5000
এই নম্বরে HealthServe-এর হেল্পলাইনে কল করতে ভুলবেন না, এটি ২৪ ঘন্টা খোলা থাকে।  
One Physio এবং আমাদের স্পোর্টিং অভিবাসী ভাইদেরকে বিশেষ ধন্যবাদ Juel Rana,
Gaurhari Mondal 📷

body, and 3 simple strengthening exercises! 📷📷📷

ব্যায়াম  শরীর শক্তিশালী  করার জন্য শেয়ার করতে অংশ নিতে বলি!  📷📷📷 এই ভিডিওটি
কি আপনার দরকারী মনে হয় ? তাহলে  আপনার বন্ধুদের সাথে শেয়ার করুন এবং একসাথে
এটি করার চেষ্টা করুন! আপনি যদি এর পরেও ব্যথা অনুভব করেন বা সাহায্যের প্রয়োজন
হয়, তাহলে 3129 5000 এই নম্বরে HealthServe-এর হেল্পলাইনে কল করতে ভুলবেন না,
এটি ২৪ ঘন্টা খোলা থাকে। One Physio  এবং আমাদের স্পোর্টিং অভিবাসী ভাইদেরকে
বিশেষ ধন্যবাদ Juel Rana, Gaurhari Mondal 📷 ---- Are you feeling back pain? We
partner our volunteer physiotherapist Ernie to share 3 steps to check your
body, and 3 simple strengthening exercises! 📷📷📷 Found this video useful? Share
it with your friends and try these together! If you still feel pain or need
help, remember to call HealthServe’s 24-hour helpline at 3129 5000. Special
thanks to One Physio and our sporting migrant brothers Juel Rana, Gaurhari
Mondal 📷 #MigrantMatters #HealthServeTips #CaringforYourHeart #health
#mentalhealth #wellness")

[![சொந்த நாட்டை விட்டு, வேறு ஒரு நாட்டில் வாழ்க்கையை வழிநடத்துவது சவாலானது
மற்றும் ஒருவரை பெரும்பாலும் தனிமைப்படுத்த வாய்ப்பு உள்ளது.  இந்த
#internationalmenshealthweek, ஹெல்த்சர்வின் புலம்பெயர்ந்த நண்பர்களைக் கொண்ட
எங்கள் மூன்று-அத்தியாய தொடரான #MigrantMatters -யின் முதல் அத்தியாயத்தை நாங்கள்
வெளியிடுகிறோம். அவர்கள் பயணித்த வாழ்க்கைப் பாதைகள் கடினமானவை, மேலும் அவர்களின்
ஆழ்ந்த தனிப்பட்ட கதைகளை எங்களுடனும், மற்றும் எங்கள் மத்தியில் உள்ள
பல்லாயிரக்கணக்கான குறைந்த ஊதியம் பெறும் புலம்பெயர்ந்த தொழிலாளர்களுடனும்,
பகிர்ந்துக் கொண்ட அவர்களுக்கு நாங்கள் நன்றி தெரிவிக்கிறோம்.  📞புலம்பெயர்ந்த
தொழிலாளி ஒருவரைப் பற்றி உங்களுக்குத் தெரிந்தால், அவர்களுடன் பேசுவதற்கு யாராவது
தேவைப்படலாம், 3129 5000 என்ற எண்ணில் HealthServe-யை அழைக்கவும்.    தாயகத்தில்
தங்களுடைய குடும்பங்களுக்கு உதவ தன்னலமின்றியும் அயராது உழைக்கும் புலம்பெயர்ந்த
சகோதரர்கள் அனைவருக்கும் தந்தையர் தின நல்வாழ்த்துக்கள் 👨❤️ அடுத்த வார இறுதியில்

Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  This
#InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode series
#MigrantMatters, featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan,
Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are grateful to them
for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and the tens of
thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.   📞If you know of a
migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.

and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  Stay tuned for the

\-----  
Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This #InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode
series [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s
migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan, Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been
rough, and we are grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal
stories with us and the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our
midst.  
  
📞If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  
  
Stay tuned for the next episode of [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters)
next weekend!

**](/tag/migrantmatters)]( "বাড়ি থেকে দূরের জীবন  চ্যালেঞ্জিং এবং প্রায়শই
পরিবারের সাথে যোগাযোগ বিচ্ছিন্ন হতে পারে। এই #InternationalMensHealthWeek,
আমরা HealthServe-এর অভিবাসী বন্ধুদের Imon , Samim,  Juel Rana  সমন্বিত
MigrantMatters-এর তিন পর্বের সিরিজের প্রথমটি উন্মোচন করেছি ।  তাদের রাস্তাগুলি
রুক্ষ ছিল, এবং আমাদের সাথে তাদের গভীর ব্যক্তিগত গল্প শেয়ার করা এবং আমাদের মাঝে
হাজার হাজার স্বল্প বেতনের অভিবাসী শ্রমিকদের সাহসের সাথে ভাগ করে নেওয়ার জন্য
আমরা তাদের কাছে কৃতজ্ঞ। ☎️আপনি যদি একজন অভিবাসী কর্মী সম্পর্কে জানেন যার সাথে
কথা বলার জন্য কারো প্রয়োজন হতে পারে, তাহলে 3129 5000 নম্বরে HealthServe-এ কল
করুন। আমাদের সমস্ত অভিবাসী ভাইদের জন্য বাবা দিবসের শুভেচ্ছা , যারা তাদের
পরিবারের জন্য নিঃস্বার্থভাবে এবং নিরলসভাবে কাজ করে।👨🏻❤️ পরের সপ্তাহান্তে
#MigrantMatters  -এর পরবর্তী পর্বের জন্য সাথে থাকুন! ----------- Navigating
life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating. This
#Internationalmenshealthweek , we unveil the first of our three-episode series
#MigrantMatters, featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Imon , Samim, and
Juel Rana. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are grateful to them
for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and the tens of
thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst. ☎️ If you know of a
migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨🏻❤️ Stay tuned for the
next episode of #MigrantMattersnext weekend! #MigrantMatters #HealthServeTips
#CaringforYourHeart #health #mentalhealth #wellness")

management techniques 💪🏽 We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends

“Mental health is a universal human right.” 🤝  
  
To remind our migrant brothers of their universal human right, we got together
with close to 50 of our Peer Support Leaders (PSLs) last Sunday to commemorate
World Mental Health Day!  
  
Through engaging and thought-provoking activities planned by our mental health
team, our PSLs expanded their understanding about resilience and useful stress
management techniques 💪🏽  
  
We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends stepping forward as volunteers,
empowering their fellow brothers. Watch on for a glimpse of our joyous day 🥰!  
  
#migrantworkers #community #HealthServe #WorldMentalHealthDay2023
#WorldMentalHealthDay #mentalhealthawareness #mentalhealth #resilience](

[![Curious how a Peer Support Leader \(PSL\) training programme for migrant
workers looks like? Join us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather
every week to conduct uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant
friends, right in their dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬
#DidYouKnow that HealthServe kicked off its first PSL training – the first of
its kind in Singapore for migrant workers – in 2021? To date, we’ve equipped
close to 1100 PSLs who serve as crucial first detectors of distress signs on
the ground. Huge shoutout to our community of participants, supportive
employers and committed volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟 #HealthServe
#CommunityCare #mentalhealth #healthcare #migrantworkers #behindhealthserve

[ Curious how a Peer Support Leader (PSL) training programme for migrant
workers looks like?  
  
Join us for a sneak peek behind the scenes where we gather every week to
conduct uplifting psychoeducation sessions for our migrant friends, right in
their dorms or RCs, delivered in their languages 💬  
  
[**#DidYouKnow **](/tag/didyouknow) that HealthServe kicked off its first PSL
training – the first of its kind in Singapore for migrant workers – in 2021?
To date, we’ve equipped close to 1100 PSLs who serve as crucial first
detectors of distress signs on the ground.  
  
Huge shoutout to our community of participants, supportive employers and
committed volunteers, staff and interns! 🌟

[![Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers?  🏥✨
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need. For the past 16
years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill low-wage migrant
workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So thankful for
their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff, volunteers and
interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️ 🕡Please keep in mind
that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and Thursday from 6:30 pm to
9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at 5.30pm on a first come first serve basis.
#HealthServe  #Clinic  #CommunityCare  #healthcare  #migrantworkers created by
HealthServe with HealthServe's original sound - HealthServe](https://p16-sign-

[ Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers? 🏥✨  
  
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need.  
  
For the past 16 years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill
low-wage migrant workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So
thankful for their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff,
volunteers and interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️  
  
🕡Please keep in mind that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and
Thursday from 6:30 pm to 9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at 5.30pm on a first
come first serve basis.

[**#CommunityCare **](/tag/communitycare) [**#healthcare **](/tag/healthcare)
[**#migrantworkers **](/tag/migrantworkers)]( "Curious what goes on behind a
community clinic for migrant workers?  🏥✨ Come along as we peel back the
curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang, where a community comes together
to care for those in need. For the past 16 years, the HealthServe clinic has
stayed open to support ill low-wage migrant workers who did not have access to
affordable healthcare. So thankful for their trust in us, and our committed
team of clinic staff, volunteers and interns who keep our clinic running day
in night out. ❤️ 🕡Please keep in mind that our clinic is open every Tuesday,
Wednesday, and Thursday from 6:30 pm to 9:30 pm. Tokens are given out at

[ আপনি কি আপনার পিঠে ব্যথা অনুভব করছেন?  
আমরা আমাদের স্বেচ্ছাসেবক ফিজিওথেরাপিস্ট ERNIE কে আপনার শরীর পরীক্ষা করার জন্য
৩ টি ধাপ এবং ৩ টি সহজ ব্যায়াম শরীর শক্তিশালী করার জন্য শেয়ার করতে অংশ নিতে
বলি! 📷📷📷  
এই ভিডিওটি কি আপনার দরকারী মনে হয় ? তাহলে আপনার বন্ধুদের সাথে শেয়ার করুন এবং
একসাথে এটি করার চেষ্টা করুন!  
আপনি যদি এর পরেও ব্যথা অনুভব করেন বা সাহায্যের প্রয়োজন হয়, তাহলে 3129 5000
এই নম্বরে HealthServe-এর হেল্পলাইনে কল করতে ভুলবেন না, এটি ২৪ ঘন্টা খোলা থাকে।  
One Physio এবং আমাদের স্পোর্টিং অভিবাসী ভাইদেরকে বিশেষ ধন্যবাদ Juel Rana,
Gaurhari Mondal 📷  
\----  
Are you feeling back pain?  
We partner our volunteer physiotherapist Ernie to share 3 steps to check your
body, and 3 simple strengthening exercises! 📷📷📷  
Found this video useful? Share it with your friends and try these together!  
If you still feel pain or need help, remember to call HealthServe’s 24-hour
helpline at 3129 5000.  
Special thanks to One Physio and our sporting migrant brothers Juel Rana,
Gaurhari Mondal  
📷

மற்றும் ஒருவரை பெரும்பாலும் தனிமைப்படுத்த வாய்ப்பு உள்ளது.  இந்த

பகிர்ந்துக் கொண்ட அவர்களுக்கு நாங்கள் நன்றி தெரிவிக்கிறோம்.  📞புலம்பெயர்ந்த
தொழிலாளி ஒருவரைப் பற்றி உங்களுக்குத் தெரிந்தால், அவர்களுடன் பேசுவதற்கு யாராவது

Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  This
#InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode series
#MigrantMatters, featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan,
Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are grateful to them
for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and the tens of
thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.   📞If you know of a
migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  Stay tuned for the
next episode of #MigrantMatters next weekend!  #MigrantMatters

\-----  
Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This #InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode
series [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s
migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan, Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been
rough, and we are grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal
stories with us and the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our
midst.  
  
📞If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  
  
Stay tuned for the next episode of [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters)
next weekend!

সাথে তাদের গভীর ব্যক্তিগত গল্প শেয়ার করা এবং আমাদের মাঝে হাজার হাজার স্বল্প
বেতনের অভিবাসী শ্রমিকদের সাহসের সাথে ভাগ করে নেওয়ার জন্য আমরা তাদের কাছে
কৃতজ্ঞ। ☎️আপনি যদি একজন অভিবাসী কর্মী সম্পর্কে জানেন যার সাথে কথা বলার জন্য
কারো প্রয়োজন হতে পারে, তাহলে 3129 5000 নম্বরে HealthServe-এ কল করুন। আমাদের
সমস্ত অভিবাসী ভাইদের জন্য বাবা দিবসের শুভেচ্ছা , যারা তাদের পরিবারের জন্য
নিঃস্বার্থভাবে এবং নিরলসভাবে কাজ করে।👨🏻❤️ পরের সপ্তাহান্তে #MigrantMatters

বিচ্ছিন্ন হতে পারে।  
  
এই [**#InternationalMensHealthWeek **](/tag/internationalmenshealthweek), আমরা
HealthServe-এর অভিবাসী বন্ধুদের Imon , Samim, Juel Rana সমন্বিত
MigrantMatters-এর তিন পর্বের সিরিজের প্রথমটি উন্মোচন করেছি । তাদের রাস্তাগুলি
রুক্ষ ছিল, এবং আমাদের সাথে তাদের গভীর ব্যক্তিগত গল্প শেয়ার করা এবং আমাদের মাঝে
হাজার হাজার স্বল্প বেতনের অভিবাসী শ্রমিকদের সাহসের সাথে ভাগ করে নেওয়ার জন্য
আমরা তাদের কাছে কৃতজ্ঞ।  
  
☎️আপনি যদি একজন অভিবাসী কর্মী সম্পর্কে জানেন যার সাথে কথা বলার জন্য কারো
প্রয়োজন হতে পারে, তাহলে 3129 5000 নম্বরে HealthServe-এ কল করুন।  
  
আমাদের সমস্ত অভিবাসী ভাইদের জন্য বাবা দিবসের শুভেচ্ছা , যারা তাদের পরিবারের
জন্য নিঃস্বার্থভাবে এবং নিরলসভাবে কাজ করে।👨🏻❤️  
  
পরের সপ্তাহান্তে [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters) -এর পরবর্তী
পর্বের জন্য সাথে থাকুন!  
\-----------  
Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This [**#Internationalmenshealthweek **](/tag/internationalmenshealthweek) ,
we unveil the first of our three-episode series [**#MigrantMatters
**](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Imon ,
Samim, and Juel Rana. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are
grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and
the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.  
  
☎️ If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨🏻❤️  
  
Stay tuned for the next episode of [**#MigrantMatters
**](/tag/migrantmatters)next weekend!  
  
#MigrantMatters [**#HealthServeTips **](/tag/healthservetips)

পরিবারের সাথে যোগাযোগ বিচ্ছিন্ন হতে পারে। এই #InternationalMensHealthWeek,
আমরা HealthServe-এর অভিবাসী বন্ধুদের Imon , Samim,  Juel Rana  সমন্বিত

হাজার হাজার স্বল্প বেতনের অভিবাসী শ্রমিকদের সাহসের সাথে ভাগ করে নেওয়ার জন্য

“Mental health is a universal human right.” 🤝  
  
To remind our migrant brothers of their universal human right, we got together
with close to 50 of our Peer Support Leaders (PSLs) last Sunday to commemorate
World Mental Health Day!  
  
Through engaging and thought-provoking activities planned by our mental health
team, our PSLs expanded their understanding about resilience and useful stress
management techniques 💪🏽  
  
We are deeply moved to see our migrant friends stepping forward as volunteers,
empowering their fellow brothers. Watch on for a glimpse of our joyous day 🥰!

[[ **#DidYouKnow **](/tag/didyouknow) that the number of migrant callers to
HealthServe’s crisis helpline doubled to 4,000 in 2022?  
  
Manned by trained crisis helpline specialists and volunteers, the round-the-
clock service serves to provide a safe space for migrant workers in distress.  
  
This World Suicide Prevention Day, we asked our counsellor Durga about one
call that affected her the most.  
  
You can lend a listening ear too👂🏽: https://healthserve.org.sg/volunteer

to HealthServe’s crisis helpline doubled to 4,000 in 2022? Manned by trained
crisis helpline specialists and volunteers, the round-the-clock service serves
to provide a safe space for migrant workers in distress. This World Suicide
Prevention Day, we asked our counsellor Durga about one call that affected her
the most. You can lend a listening ear too👂🏽:
https://healthserve.org.sg/volunteer #WorldSuicidePreventionDay #Community
#Mentalhealth #HealthServe #Suicideprevention")

[![Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers?  🏥✨
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need. For the past 16
years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill low-wage migrant
workers who did not have access to affordable healthcare. So thankful for
their trust in us, and our committed team of clinic staff, volunteers and
interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️ 🕡Please keep in mind
that our clinic is open every Tuesday, Wednesday, and Thursday from 6:30 pm to

[ Curious what goes on behind a community clinic for migrant workers? 🏥✨  
  
Come along as we peel back the curtain at HealthServe’s clinic in Geylang,
where a community comes together to care for those in need.  
  
For the past 16 years, the HealthServe clinic has stayed open to support ill

volunteers and interns who keep our clinic running day in night out. ❤️

come first serve basis.

Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  This
#InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode series
#MigrantMatters, featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan,
Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are grateful to them
for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and the tens of
thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.   📞If you know of a
migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️  Stay tuned for the
next episode of #MigrantMatters next weekend!  #MigrantMatters

Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This #InternationalMensHealthWeek, we unveil the first of our three-episode
series [**#MigrantMatters **](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s
migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan, Selvaraj. Their roads traveled have been
rough, and we are grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal
stories with us and the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our
midst.  
  
📞If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨❤️

next weekend!

வழிநடத்துவது சவாலானது மற்றும் ஒருவரை பெரும்பாலும் தனிமைப்படுத்த வாய்ப்பு
உள்ளது.  இந்த  #internationalmenshealthweek, ஹெல்த்சர்வின் புலம்பெயர்ந்த
நண்பர்களைக் கொண்ட எங்கள் மூன்று-அத்தியாய தொடரான #MigrantMatters -யின் முதல்
அத்தியாயத்தை நாங்கள் வெளியிடுகிறோம். அவர்கள் பயணித்த வாழ்க்கைப் பாதைகள்
கடினமானவை, மேலும் அவர்களின் ஆழ்ந்த தனிப்பட்ட கதைகளை எங்களுடனும், மற்றும்
எங்கள் மத்தியில் உள்ள  பல்லாயிரக்கணக்கான குறைந்த ஊதியம் பெறும் புலம்பெயர்ந்த
தொழிலாளர்களுடனும், பகிர்ந்துக் கொண்ட அவர்களுக்கு நாங்கள் நன்றி தெரிவிக்கிறோம்.
📞புலம்பெயர்ந்த தொழிலாளி ஒருவரைப் பற்றி உங்களுக்குத் தெரிந்தால், அவர்களுடன்
பேசுவதற்கு யாராவது தேவைப்படலாம், 3129 5000 என்ற எண்ணில் HealthServe-யை
அழைக்கவும்.    தாயகத்தில் தங்களுடைய குடும்பங்களுக்கு உதவ தன்னலமின்றியும்
அயராது உழைக்கும் புலம்பெயர்ந்த சகோதரர்கள் அனைவருக்கும் தந்தையர் தின
நல்வாழ்த்துக்கள் 👨❤️ அடுத்த வார இறுதியில் #MigrantMatters -யின் அடுத்த
அத்தியாயத்தை பார்க்க காத்திருங்கள்! ----- Navigating life in a new country can
be challenging and often isolating.  This #InternationalMensHealthWeek, we
unveil the first of our three-episode series #MigrantMatters, featuring
HealthServe’s migrant friends Amaran, Pandiyan, Selvaraj. Their roads traveled
have been rough, and we are grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply
personal stories with us and the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers
in our midst.   📞If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk
to, call HealthServe at 3129 5000.  P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our
migrant brothers who work selflessly and tirelessly to provide for their
families back home 👨❤️  Stay tuned for the next episode of #MigrantMatters
next weekend!  #MigrantMatters #HealthServeTips #CaringforYourHeart #health
#mentalhealth #wellness")

[![বাড়ি থেকে দূরের জীবন  চ্যালেঞ্জিং এবং প্রায়শই পরিবারের সাথে যোগাযোগ
বিচ্ছিন্ন হতে পারে। এই #InternationalMensHealthWeek, আমরা HealthServe-এর
অভিবাসী বন্ধুদের Imon , Samim,  Juel Rana  সমন্বিত MigrantMatters-এর তিন
পর্বের সিরিজের প্রথমটি উন্মোচন করেছি ।  তাদের রাস্তাগুলি রুক্ষ ছিল, এবং আমাদের
সাথে তাদের গভীর ব্যক্তিগত গল্প শেয়ার করা এবং আমাদের মাঝে হাজার হাজার স্বল্প
বেতনের অভিবাসী শ্রমিকদের সাহসের সাথে ভাগ করে নেওয়ার জন্য আমরা তাদের কাছে
কৃতজ্ঞ। ☎️আপনি যদি একজন অভিবাসী কর্মী সম্পর্কে জানেন যার সাথে কথা বলার জন্য
কারো প্রয়োজন হতে পারে, তাহলে 3129 5000 নম্বরে HealthServe-এ কল করুন। আমাদের
সমস্ত অভিবাসী ভাইদের জন্য বাবা দিবসের শুভেচ্ছা , যারা তাদের পরিবারের জন্য
নিঃস্বার্থভাবে এবং নিরলসভাবে কাজ করে।👨🏻❤️ পরের সপ্তাহান্তে #MigrantMatters
-এর পরবর্তী পর্বের জন্য সাথে থাকুন! ----------- Navigating life in a new
country can be challenging and often isolating. This

Juel Rana. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are grateful to them
for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and the tens of

বিচ্ছিন্ন হতে পারে।  
  
এই [**#InternationalMensHealthWeek **](/tag/internationalmenshealthweek), আমরা
HealthServe-এর অভিবাসী বন্ধুদের Imon , Samim, Juel Rana সমন্বিত
MigrantMatters-এর তিন পর্বের সিরিজের প্রথমটি উন্মোচন করেছি । তাদের রাস্তাগুলি
রুক্ষ ছিল, এবং আমাদের সাথে তাদের গভীর ব্যক্তিগত গল্প শেয়ার করা এবং আমাদের মাঝে
হাজার হাজার স্বল্প বেতনের অভিবাসী শ্রমিকদের সাহসের সাথে ভাগ করে নেওয়ার জন্য
আমরা তাদের কাছে কৃতজ্ঞ।  
  
☎️আপনি যদি একজন অভিবাসী কর্মী সম্পর্কে জানেন যার সাথে কথা বলার জন্য কারো
প্রয়োজন হতে পারে, তাহলে 3129 5000 নম্বরে HealthServe-এ কল করুন।  
  
আমাদের সমস্ত অভিবাসী ভাইদের জন্য বাবা দিবসের শুভেচ্ছা , যারা তাদের পরিবারের
জন্য নিঃস্বার্থভাবে এবং নিরলসভাবে কাজ করে।👨🏻❤️

\-----------  
Navigating life in a new country can be challenging and often isolating.  
  
This [**#Internationalmenshealthweek **](/tag/internationalmenshealthweek) ,
we unveil the first of our three-episode series [**#MigrantMatters
**](/tag/migrantmatters), featuring HealthServe’s migrant friends Imon ,
Samim, and Juel Rana. Their roads traveled have been rough, and we are
grateful to them for bravely sharing their deeply personal stories with us and
the tens of thousands of low-wage migrant workers in our midst.  
  
☎️ If you know of a migrant worker who may need someone to talk to, call
HealthServe at 3129 5000.  
  
P.S. A very happy Fathers' Day to all our migrant brothers who work selflessly
and tirelessly to provide for their families back home 👨🏻❤️  
  
Stay tuned for the next episode of [**#MigrantMatters
**](/tag/migrantmatters)next weekend!

## Seeking assistance for a migrant worker?

### +65 3129 5000

HealthServe 24-hour Helpline

Call HealthServe’s 24-hour helpline or email us at:
